function	script	F_tt	{
	if (compare(strnpcinfo(2),"main")) end;
	set .@w$,(charat(strnpcinfo(4),6))+((getstrlen(strnpcinfo(4)) > 9)?(substr(strnpcinfo(4),8,9)):(charat(strnpcinfo(4),getstrlen(strnpcinfo(4))-1)));
	return .@w$;
}

-	script	entrance#tt_main	-1,{
	end;

OnEnable:
	enablenpc();
	enablewaitingroomevent strnpcinfo(0);
	end;

OnStartArena:
	if (compare(strnpcinfo(2),"n1")) {
		set .@in$, "n";
		set .@in, 1;
	} else {
		set .@in$,(compare(strnpcinfo(1),"Expert"))?"e":"n";
		if (compare(strnpcinfo(1),"4")) set .@in, 4;
		if (compare(strnpcinfo(1),"8")) set .@in, 8;
		if (compare(strnpcinfo(1),"16")) set .@in, 16;
	}
	warpwaitingpc "turbo_"+.@in$+"_"+.@in,298,161;
	donpcevent "Broadcast#"+.@in$+.@in+"::OnEnable";
	disablewaitingroomevent strnpcinfo(0);
	end;
	
OnInit:
	if (compare(strnpcinfo(0),"main")) end;
	if (compare(strnpcinfo(2),"n1")) {
		waitingroom "Solo Mode",60,"Solo Mode#n1::OnStartArena",1,1000,10;
	} else {
		if (compare(strnpcinfo(1),"4")) set .@in, 4;
		if (compare(strnpcinfo(1),"8")) set .@in, 8;
		if (compare(strnpcinfo(1),"16")) set .@in, 16;
		waitingroom strnpcinfo(1),60,strnpcinfo(0)+"::OnStartArena",.@in,1000,10;
	}
	enablewaitingroomevent strnpcinfo(0);
	end;
}

turbo_e_4,298,167,0	script	Point#tt_main	-1,15,15,{
	end;

OnTouch_:
	if (tt_point < 28999) {
		set tt_point,tt_point+2;
		warp strnpcinfo(4),59,364;
	}
	else
		warp strnpcinfo(4),59,364;
	end;
	
OnInit:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	disablenpc "Point Give-Away Guy#"+.@w$;
	end;
}

	end;

	end;

OnTimer44000:

OnTimer49000:

	donpcevent "hunting#"+.@w$+"::OnEnable";

	end;

	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	disablenpc "Broadcast#"+.@w$;
	end;
}

	if (strnpcinfo(4) == "turbo_n_1") {
		donpcevent "Solo Mode#n1::OnEnable";
	} else {
		donpcevent RName(.@w$)+"::OnEnable";
	}
	enablenpc "No_Unfair_Start#"+.@w$+"-1";
	enablenpc "No_Unfair_Start#"+.@w$+"-2";
	donpcevent "snake#"+.@w$+"::OnReset";
	donpcevent "hunting#"+.@w$+"::OnReset";
	disablenpc "bing2#"+.@w$;
	disablenpc "Winner Helper#TBT_"+.@w$;
	enablenpc "#cos_"+.@w$+"_end";
	enablenpc "Notice_Maker1#TBT_"+.@w$;
	enablenpc "Notice_Maker3#TBT_"+.@w$;
	enablenpc "Notice_Maker4#TBT_"+.@w$;
	enablenpc "Disposable_Switch#"+.@w$;
	disablenpc "Flasher_Exit_1#"+.@w$;
	disablenpc "Flasher_Exit_2#"+.@w$;
	end;
	
OnInit:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	disablenpc "Master#"+.@w$;
	end;
	
	function	RName	{
		.@string$ = getarg(0);
		.@s = ( getstrlen(.@string$) > 2 ? substr(.@string$,1,2) : charat(.@string$,getstrlen(.@string$)-1) );
		set .@rn$,((compare(strnpcinfo(4),"_e_"+.@s))?"Expert mode":"Normal mode")+" - "+.@s+" person";
		return .@rn$;
	}
}

-	script	cos_end#tt_main	01,{
	function	GetNumber;
OnTouch_:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	if (.@w$ == "n1") set $@end_time,gettimetick(0);
	mapannounce strnpcinfo(4),strcharinfo(0) +" has just arrived at the Finish Line! Congratulations!",bc_map,"0xFFFF00";
	if (.@w$ != "n1") {
		setd "$ttnames$["+GetNumber(.@w$)+"]",strcharinfo(0);
		donpcevent "Turbo Track Guide::OnWin_"+.@w$;
	}
	warp strnpcinfo(4),384,161;
	if (.@w$ == "e4" || .@w$ == "n4" || .@w$ == "n1") {
		if (.@w$ == "e4") {
			donpcevent "Winner Helper#TBT_"+.@w$+"::OnEnable";
		} else {
			donpcevent "Guide#TBT_"+.@w$+"::OnEnable";
		}
		donpcevent "Master#"+.@w$+"::OnDisable";
		disablenpc "Broadcast#"+.@w$;
	} else {
		if (.@w$ == "e8" || .@w$ == "n8") setarray .@pts, 28951,50;
		if (.@w$ == "e16" || .@w$ == "n16") setarray .@pts, 28941,60;
		if (tt_point < .@pts[0]) set tt_point,tt_point+.@pts[1];
		warp strnpcinfo(4),384,161;
		enablenpc "Winner Helper#TBT_"+.@w$;
		enablenpc "#cos_"+.@w$+"_end2";
	}
	disablenpc "#cos_"+.@w$+"_end";
	end;
	
	function	GetNumber	{
		setarray .@w_n$[1], "n4","n8","n16","e4","e8","e16";
		for (set .@i, 1; .@i <= getarraysize(.@w_n$); set .@i, .@i + 1) {
			if (getarg(0) == .@w_n$[.@i]) 
				return .@i;
		}		
	}
	
OnInit:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	enablenpc "#cos_"+.@w$+"_end";
	end;
}

OnEnable:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	enablenpc "Winner Helper#TBT_"+.@w$;
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer4000:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	mapannounce strnpcinfo(4),"This is the ending broadcast for Turbo Track "+RName(.@w$)+".",bc_map,"0x33FF66";
	end;

OnTimer8000:
	mapannounce strnpcinfo(4),"For smooth game play, the game will end in approximately 1 minute.",bc_map,"0x33FF66";
	end;

OnTimer12000:
	mapannounce strnpcinfo(4),"At that time, a Warp portal will open.",bc_map,"0x33FF66";
	end;

OnTimer16000:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	if (compare(.@w$,"4")) mapannounce strnpcinfo(4),"Players in the arena must be ready to leave through the Warp Portal.",bc_map,"0x33FF66";
	end;

OnTimer20000:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	if (compare(.@w$,"4"))
		mapannounce strnpcinfo(4),"In the meantime, winners must proceed to receive their rewards as soon as possible.",bc_map,"0x33FF66";
	else
		mapannounce strnpcinfo(4),"Players within the arena must be in ready to enter the warp.",bc_map,"0x33FF66";
	end;

OnTimer24000:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	if (compare(.@w$,"4")) mapannounce strnpcinfo(4),"Thank you for visiting Al De Baran Turbo Track.",bc_map,"0x33FF66";
	end;

OnTimer25000:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");

	end;

	function	RName	{
		.@string$ = getarg(0);
		.@s = ( getstrlen(.@string$) > 2 ? substr(.@string$,1,2) : charat(.@string$,getstrlen(.@string$)-1) );
		set .@rn$,((compare(strnpcinfo(4),"_e_"+.@s))?"Expert mode":"Normal mode")+" - "+.@s+" person";
		return .@rn$;
	}
	
OnInit:
	set .@w$,callfunc("F_tt");
	disablenpc "Winner Helper#TBT_"+.@w$;
	end;
}

turbo_n_1,384,167,1	script	Guide#TBT_n1	47,{
	set .@hour_start,$@start_time / 10000;
	set .@min_start,(($@start_time % 10000) / 100);
	set .@sec_start,$@start_time % 100;
	set .@hour_end,$@end_time / 10000;
	set .@min_end,(($@end_time % 10000) / 100);
	set .@sec_end,$@end_time % 100;
	if (hour_start == 23 && hour_end == 0) set .@hour_end,24;
	set .@st_to_sec,((.@hour_start * 3600) + (.@min_start * 60) + (.@sec_start));
	set .@et_to_sec,((.@hour_end * 3600) + (.@min_end * 60) + (.@sec_end));
	set .@record_time,(.@et_to_sec - .@st_to_sec);
	set .@record_hour,.@record_time / 3600;
	set .@record_min,((.@record_time % 3600) / 60);

		next;

		mes "在渦輪軌道上。";
		mes "您將被指導";

		end;
	}
	else {

		set .@gap,$ttranks[0] - .@record_time;

			mes "門戶，隱藏，隱身，隱身，治愈，冰牆，狂歡，大教堂，庇護和長矛發電機。";
			next;
			//this appears supposed to fall through.
		case 5:
			mes "【渦輪賽道指南】";
			mes "請享受你的";
			mes "在Al de Baran的時間";
			mes "渦輪軌道。謝謝~";
			close;
		}
	}

OnInit:
	// This will only ever be run ONCE!
	// Unless you eradicate the variable.
	//
	// This OnInit initiallizes and sets the starting
	// data for the Turbo Track's "Record" Logs.
	// WARNING/ATTENTION: DO NOT MODIFY ANY OF THE DATA.
	// DOING SO WILL CAUSE INTERNAL PROBLEMS IN THE SCRIPT.
	if ($ttnames$[0] == "") {
		setarray $ttnames$[0],"Breezy Havana";	// Solo Mode/Time Attack
		setarray $ttnames$[1],"RS125";	// Normal 4 Player
		setarray $ttnames$[2],"Hollgrehenn";	// Normal 8 Players
		setarray $ttnames$[3],"Antonio";	// Noomal 16 Players

		setarray $ttnames$[4],"Aragham";	// Expert 4 Players
		setarray $ttnames$[5],"Kafra Jasmine";	// Expert 8 Players
		setarray $ttnames$[6],"Chris";	// Expert 16 Players

		setarray $ttnames$[7],"Breezy Havana";	// Honor Place 1
		setarray $ttnames$[8],"RS125";	// Honor Place 2

		setarray $ttnames$[9],"Breezy Havana";	// Top 1
		setarray $ttnames$[10],"Nari";	// Top 2
		setarray $ttnames$[11],"Senorita Sylvia";	// Top 3
		setarray $ttnames$[12],"Joo Jahk";	// Top 4
		setarray $ttnames$[13],"RS125";	// Top 5

		setarray $ttranks[0],999999,0,0,0,0,0;
	}
	end;

	end;

	end;

			mes "您的渦輪軌跡點。";
			next;
			switch(select("卡夫拉免費門票 交通:5級魔法捲軸:經驗值:3克拉鑽石:禮盒:速度藥水:取消。")) {
			case 1:

				}

				mes "[項目交換助手]";
				mes "此項目交換";
				mes "提供服務";
				mes "給你...";
				next;
				mes "[項目交換助手]";
				mes "此項目交換服務";
				mes "是由Kafra帶給您的";
				mes "公司，鐵匠協會";
				mes "和comodo賭場和";
				mes "al de Baran Guild城堡";
				mes "管理Luina。";
				close;
			}
		case 2:
			mes "[項目交換助手]";
			mes "渦輪軌道可以是";
			mes "轉換為競技場點。";
			mes "您最多可以節省";
			mes "^4D4DFF29,000渦輪軌道點。";
			next;
			mes "[項目交換助手]";
			mes "在達到最大值之前";
			mes "渦輪軌道點的數量，";
			mes "你可能想花一些";
			mes "他們中的";
			mes "贏得渦輪賽道比賽后，獲得了積分獎勵。";
			close;
		}
	}
}

turbo_room,106,117,3	script	Point Manager#tt	833,{
	mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
	mes "再會。";
	mes "你喜歡你的嗎";
	mes "在渦輪軌道上的時間？";
	mes "我怎麼可能";
	mes "協助？";
	next;
	switch(select("檢查點數:兌換點數:^660000兌換信息^000000")) {
	case 1:
		mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
		mes "" + strcharinfo(0) + ",";
		mes "您目前有";
		mes "" + tt_point + " Turbo Track Points";
		mes "和" + arena_point + " Arena Points.";
		close;
	case 2:
		mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
		mes "" + strcharinfo(0) + ",";
		mes "您目前有";
		mes "" + tt_point + " Turbo Track Points";
		mes "和" + arena_point + " Arena Points.";
		next;
		mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
		mes "請從以下競技場點轉換中進行選擇。轉換超過";
		mes "同時，您的10個競技場點";
		mes "只能轉換競技場點";
		mes "在10 ^000000的 ^4d4dfffmultiples中。";
		next;
		switch(select("2 AP -> 1 TTP:4 AP -> 2 TTP:6 AP -> 3 TTP:8 AP -> 4 TTP:10 AP 或更多:取消")) {
		case 1:
			callsub S_ExchangePoints,28999,2,1;
		case 2:
			callsub S_ExchangePoints,28998,4,2;
		case 3:
			callsub S_ExchangePoints,28997,6,2;
		case 4:
			callsub S_ExchangePoints,28996,8,4;
		case 5:
			mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
			mes "請輸入您希望將10個競技場轉換為渦輪軌跡點的次數。您可能輸入的最大價值";
			mes "為20。要取消，輸入'^3355ff0^000000。";
			next;
			input .@input;
			if (.@input <= 0) {
				mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
				mes "你有";
				mes "取消";
				mes "您的要求。";
				close;
			}
			else if (.@input > 20) {
				mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
				mes "您的請求超出了";
				mes "最大限制。請";
				mes "輸入不超過20的值。";
				close;
			}
			else {
				set .@want_point1,10 * .@input;
				set .@want_point,5 * .@input;
				set .@my_turbo_all,tt_point+.@want_point;
				set .@my_arena_all,arena_point-.@want_point1;
				if (.@my_turbo_all > 28999) {
					mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
					mes "不幸的是，如果我們進行點轉換，則您的渦輪軌道點將超過最大限制。請花更多";
					mes "在使用此服務之前，您的渦輪軌道點。謝謝。";
					close;
				}
				if (.@my_arena_all < 0) {
					mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
					mes "對不起，但是你願意";
					mes "沒有足夠的競技場積分";
					mes "執行此渦輪軌道";
					mes "點轉換。";
					close;
				}
				else {
					mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
					mes "您已經轉換了";
					mes "10個競技場點";
					mes "渦輪軌跡點" + .@input + " times.";
					mes "總共" + .@want_point1 + " Arena Points";
					mes "已轉換為";
					mes "" + .@want_point +" Turbo Track Points.";
					set arena_point,.@my_arena_all; //arena_point
					set tt_point,.@my_turbo_all;
					next;
					mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
					mes "" + strcharinfo(0) + ",";
					mes "你現在有";
					mes "^00688B" + tt_point + "^000000 Turbo Track Points";
					mes "和 ^4682b4" + arena_point + "^000000 Arena Points.";
					mes "謝謝您的讚助。";
					close;
				}
			}
		case 6:
			mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
			mes "你有";
			mes "取消";
			mes "您的要求。";
			close;
		}
	case 3:
		// There is no dialog for this option.
		// It's possible it's missing, or maybe
		// the dialog was never translated. XD
		//??
		close;
	}

S_ExchangePoints:
	if (tt_point > getarg(0)) {
		mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
		mes "不幸的是，如果我們進行點轉換，則您的渦輪軌道點將超過最大限制。請花更多";
		mes "在使用此服務之前，您的渦輪軌道點。謝謝。";
		close;
	}
	if (arena_point >= getarg(1)) {
		mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
		mes "根據要求";
		mes "2個競技場";
		mes "已轉換";
		mes "進入1個渦輪軌道點。";
		set arena_point,arena_point-getarg(1);
		set tt_point,tt_point+getarg(2);
		next;
		mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
		mes "" + strcharinfo(0) + ",";
		mes "你現在有";
		mes "^00688B" + tt_point + "^000000 Turbo Track Points";
		mes "和 ^4682b4" + arena_point + "^000000 Arena Points.";
		mes "謝謝您的讚助。";
		close;
	}
	else {
		mes "[渦輪軌跡點管理器]";
		mes "對不起，但是您沒有足夠的競技場。你需要";
		mes "至少有2個競技場的順序";
		mes "使用此服務。";
		close;
	}
}

alde_gld,183,204,0	script	en_turbo	45,1,1,{
OnTouch_:
	if (checkweight(1201,1) == 0) {
		mes "^3355FFWAIT第二秒！";
		mes "現在，您正在攜帶";
		mes "和你在一起太多。";
		mes "請在";
		mes "放置您的一些";
		mes "使用Kafra服務的事物。 ^000000";
		close;
	}
	if ((BaseJob == Job_Knight || BaseJob == Job_Crusader) && (checkriding() || checkdragon())) {
		if (MaxWeight-Weight < 20000) {
			if (!(eaclass()&EAJL_THIRD)) {
				set .@mount$,(BaseJob == Job_Knight)?"Peco Peco":"Grand Peco";
				mes "[幫手]";
				mes .@mount$+"s被禁止";
				mes "在渦輪軌道競技場。";
				mes "請從您的";
				mes .@mount$+"你會收到";
				mes "Peco Ride的免費門票";
				mes "要檢索您的"+.@mount$+".";
			} else {
				set .@mount$,(BaseJob == Job_Knight)?"Dragon":"Gryphon";
				mes "[幫手]";
				mes .@mount$+"s被禁止";
				mes "在渦輪軌道競技場。";
				mes "請從您的";
				mes .@mount$+"。您可以檢索";
				mes "外面免費。";
			}
			close2;
			warp "alde_gld",183,199;
			end;
		} else {
			if (!(eaclass()&EAJL_THIRD)) {
				setriding 0;
				getitem 7310,1; //Free_Peco_Ticket
			} else {
				if (BaseJob == Job_Knight)
					setdragon 0;
				else
					setriding 0;
			}
			warp "turbo_room",100,65;
		}
	} else if ((Class == Job_Ranger || Class == Job_Ranger_T || Class == Job_Baby_Ranger) && checkoption(Option_Wugrider)) {
		if (MaxWeight-Weight < 20000) {
			mes "[幫手]";
			mes "禁止戰爭";
			mes "在渦輪軌道競技場。";
			mes "請從您的戰爭中卸下。";
			close2;
			warp "alde_gld",183,199;
			end;
		} else {
			setoption Option_Wugrider,0;
			warp "turbo_room",100,65;
		}
	} else if ((Class == Job_Mechanic || Class == Job_Mechanic_T || Class == Job_Baby_Mechanic) && checkmadogear()) {
		if (MaxWeight-Weight < 20000) {
			mes "[幫手]";
			mes "禁止魔術齒輪";
			mes "在渦輪軌道競技場。";
			mes "請從您的";
			mes "魔術裝備。您可以檢索";
			mes "外面免費。";
			close2;
			warp "alde_gld",183,199;
			end;
		} else {
			setmadogear 0;
			warp "turbo_room",100,65;
		}
	} else
		warp "turbo_room",100,65;
	end;
}

-	script	::MountManager_turbo	-1,{
	set .@n$, "["+strnpcinfo(1)+"]";
	mes .@n$;
	if (ismounting()) {
		mes "請擺脫您正在騎的生物。";
		mes "然後再次與我交談。";
		close;
	}
	if (BaseJob == Job_Knight || BaseJob == Job_Crusader) {
		if (!(eaclass()&EAJL_THIRD)) {
			if (BaseJob == Job_Knight) {
				set .@zeny,2500;
				set .@zeny$,"2,500";
				set .@mount$,"Peco Peco";
			} else {
				set .@zeny,3500;
				set .@zeny$,"3,500";
				set .@mount$,"Grand Peco";
			}
			set .@skill,63;
			set .@skill$,"Peco Peco Ride";
			set .@riding, checkriding();
			set .@i,1;
		} else {
			if (BaseJob == Job_Knight) {
				set .@mount$,"Dragon";
				set .@skill,63;
				set .@skill$,"Dragon Training";
				set .@riding, checkdragon();
				set .@i,2;
			} else {
				set .@mount$,"Gryphon";
				set .@skill,63;
				set .@skill$,"Peco Peco Ride";
				set .@riding, checkriding();
				set .@i,1;
			}
		}
	} else if (Class == Job_Mechanic || Class == Job_Mechanic_T || Class == Job_Baby_Mechanic) {
		set .@mount$,"Magic Gear";
		set .@skill,2255;
		set .@skill$,"Magic Gear License";
		set .@riding, checkmadogear();
		set .@i,3;
	} else {
		mes "謝謝你";
		mes "參觀al de Baran的";
		mes "渦輪軌道~";
		close;
	}
	mes "歡迎，你想要嗎";
	mes "取回你"+.@mount$+"?";
	if (.@zeny) {
		mes "請讓我免費";
		mes "Peco Ride的票。你";
		mes "也可以支付租金";
		mes "的"+.@zeny$+" zeny.";
	}
	next;
	switch(select("是:取消")) {
	case 1:
		if (getskilllv(.@skill) == 0) {
			mes .@n$;
			mes "對不起，但是你";
			mes "沒有資格";
			mes "服務。請去學習";
			mes "這"+.@skill$+" skill first.";
			close;
		} else {
			if (.@riding) {
				mes .@n$;
				mes "你已經";
				mes "安裝在一個";
				mes .@mount$+"。";
				mes "謝謝~";
				close;
			} else {
				if (.@zeny) {
					if (countitem(7310) < 1 && Zeny < .@zeny) {
						mes .@n$;
						mes "對不起，但是你";
						mes "沒有免費票";
						mes "乘坐peco或"+.@zeny$+" zeny.";
						mes "使用PECO租賃服務。";
						close;
					} else {
						if (countitem(7310) > 0)
							delitem 7310,1; //Free_Peco_Ticket
						else
							set Zeny, Zeny-.@zeny;
					}
				}
				switch(.@i) {
					case 1: setriding; break;
					case 2: setdragon; break;
					case 3: setmadogear; break;
				}
				mes .@n$;
				mes "謝謝你";
				mes "您的讚助~";
				close;
			}
		}
	case 2:
		mes .@n$;
		mes "你要去嗎";
		mes "回到比賽";
		mes "渦輪軌道？";
		mes "祝你好運！";
		close;
	}
}
